# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Envoy External Authorization Bypass Controls

## Your Task

Find all C++ source files in envoyproxy/envoy that implement the ext_authz filter's bypass and passthrough logic: the per-route bypass configuration, the authorization decision caching, and the immediate response path.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the security domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2, sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367, sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6, sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2` (envoyproxy/envoy)

Depending on the response, the filter may reject or accept the client\\n327: // request. Note that in any of these events, metadata can be added, removed or overridden by the\\n328: // filter:\\n329: //\\n330: // *On authorization request*, a list of allowed request headers may be supplied. PER-ROUTE BYPASS CONFIGURATION:\\nThe FilterConfigPerRoute class (ext_authz.h) stores per-route configuration with a disabled() method that controls whether authorization checks are bypassed for specific routes. The FilterConfig class also implements filterEnabled() method that checks global filter enable/disable status via metadata matchers and runtime flags.\\n\\n2. BYPASS LOGIC FLOW:\\nIn Filter::decodeHeaders() (ext_authz.cc:226), the skip_check_ flag is set by calling getPerRouteFlags() (ext_authz.cc:810), which resolves the most specific per-route configuration. If skip_check_ is true (line 230-231), the filter immediately returns Continue, bypassing authorization checks without calling initiateCall().\\n\\n3. ROUTE CACHE CLEARING:\\nThe clearRouteCache() configuration (ext_authz.h:73) and corresponding clear_route_cache_ field (ext_authz.h:180) control whether the route cache should be invalidated when authorization responses modify request headers. This is implemented in Filter::onComplete() (ext_authz.cc:434-442) where the cache is cleared if response headers modify the request.\\n\\n4. IMMEDIATE RESPONSE PATH:\\nThe Filter::onComplete() method (ext_authz.cc:403) handles authorization responses immediately upon completion. The initiating_call_ flag (ext_authz.h:365) distinguishes between synchronous (stack-based) and asynchronous callbacks. The Response struct (common/ext_authz.h:86) contains all header mutations that can be applied immediately to both upstream and downstream responses.\\n\\n5. COMMON AUTHORIZATION HANDLING:\\nThe common ext_authz implementation provides the Response struct with comprehensive header mutation support (headers_to_add, headers_to_set, headers_to_append, headers_to_remove) for both request upstream and response downstream paths. The CheckRequestUtils class creates authorization check requests that are sent via either HTTP (RawHttpClientImpl) or gRPC (GrpcClientImpl) clients.\\n\\n6. HTTP/GRPC CLIENT IMPLEMENTATIONS:\\nRawHttpClientImpl (ext_authz_http_impl.h) and GrpcClientImpl (ext_authz_grpc_impl.h) both implement the Client interface and handle authorization responses. Their onSuccess() callbacks process the CheckResponse and trigger the immediate response path through RequestCallbacks::onComplete().\\n\\n7. NETWORK FILTER SUPPORT:\\nThe network ext_authz filter (source/extensions/filters/network/ext_authz/) provides similar bypass and decision caching mechanisms at the TCP connection level through its Config class and Filter::onComplete() implementation.\\n\\nAll per-route configuration is created via ExtAuthzFilterConfig::createRouteSpecificFilterConfigTyped() (config.cc:72), which instantiates FilterConfigPerRoute objects that allow bypassing checks at the virtual host, route, or weighted cluster level.\"\n}\n",
